\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mpu6050\_deinit()}{mpu6050\_deinit()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint8\+\_\+t mpu6050\+\_\+deinit (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group__mpu6050__basic__driver_gab9152935d0f1c91a6183aa8f398b7045}{mpu6050\+\_\+handle\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{handle }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



close the chip 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em $\ast$handle} & points to a mpu6050 handle structure \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
status code
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item 0 success
\item 1 iic deinit failed
\item 2 handle is NULL
\item 3 handle is not initialized
\item 4 enter sleep mode failed 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

none
